```java
package io.openruntimes.java.src;

import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeContext;
import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeOutput;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.HashMap;

public class Main {
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        switch (context.getReq().getQuery()["type"]) {
            case "text":
                return context.getRes().empty();
            case "json":
                HashMap<String, Object> data = new HashMap<>();
                data.put("type", "This is a JSON response");
                return context.getRes().text(data);
            case "binary"
                return context.getRes().binary(Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get("file.png")));
            case "redirect":
                return context.getRes().redirect("https://clikkle.io", 301);
            case "html":
                return context.getRes().text("<h1>This is an HTML response</h1>", 200, Map.of("content-type", "text/html"));
            default:
                return context.getRes().text("This is a text response");
        }
    }
}
```
```cpp
#include "../RuntimeResponse.h"
#include "../RuntimeRequest.h"
#include "../RuntimeOutput.h"
#include "../RuntimeContext.h"

namespace runtime {
  class Handler {
    public:
      static RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext &context) {
        std::string type = context.req.query["type"];

        if (type == "empty") {
          return context.res.empty();
        } else if (type == "json") {
          Json::Value data;
          data["type"] = "This is a JSON response";
          return context.res.text(data);
        } else if (type == "binary") {
          std::vector<char> buffer(std::istreambuf_iterator<char>(std::ifstream("file.png", std::ios::binary)), {});
          return context.res.binary(buffer)
        } else if (type == "redirect") {
          return context.res.redirect("https://clikkle.io", 301);
        } else if (type == "html") {
          Json::Value headers;
          headers["content-type"] = "text/html";
          return context.res.text("<h1>This is an HTML response</h1>", 200, headers);
        } else {
          return context.res.text("This is a text response");
        }
      }
  };
}
```
{% /multicode %}

To get the different response types, set one of the following query parameters in the [generated domain](/docs/products/functions/domains) of your function.

| Type     | Query Param     | Example                                                     |
|----------|-----------------|-------------------------------------------------------------|
| `text`     | `/?type=text`     | `https://64d4d22db370ae41a32e.fra.clikkle.run/?type=text`     |
| `json`     | `/?type=json`     | `https://64d4d22db370ae41a32e.fra.clikkle.run/?type=json`     |
| `redirect` | `/?type=redirect` | `https://64d4d22db370ae41a32e.fra.clikkle.run/?type=redirect` |
| `html`     | `/?type=html`     | `https://64d4d22db370ae41a32e.fra.clikkle.run/?type=html`     |
| `empty`    | `/`               | `https://64d4d22db370ae41a32e.fra.clikkle.run/`               |

## Logging {% #logging %}
To protect user privacy, the request and response objects are not logged to the Clikkle Console by default.

We support the spread operator across most of the languages, meaning you can write code that is more concise and flexible.

This means, to see logs or debug function executions you need to use the `log()` and `error()` methods.
These logs are only visible to developers with access to the Clikkle Console.

Here's an example of using logs and errors.

{% multicode %}
```server-nodejs
export default async ({ req, res, log, error }) => {
    const message = "This is a log, use for logging information to console";
    log("Message: ", message);
    log(`This function was called with ${req.method} method`);
    const errorMessage = "This is an error, use for logging errors to console"
    error("Error: ", errorMessage);

    return res.text("Check the Clikkle Console to see logs and errors!");
};
```
```php
<?php

return function ($context) {
    $message = "This is a log, use for logging information to console";
    $context->log("Message: ", message);
    $context->log("This function was called with " . $context->req->method . " method");
    $errorMessage = "Check the Clikkle Console to see logs and errors!"
    $context->error("Error: ", errorMessage);

    return $context->text("Check the Clikkle Console to see logs and errors!");
};
```
```python
def main(context):
    message = "This is a log, use for logging information to console"
    context.log("Message: ", message)
    context.log(f"This function was called with {context.req.method} method")
    errorMessage = "This is an error, use for logging errors to console"
    context.error("Error: ", errorMessage)

    return context.res.text("Check the Clikkle Console to see logs and errors!")
```
```ruby
def main(context)
    message = "This is a log, use for logging information to console"

    errorMessage = "This is an error, use for logging errors to console"
    context.error("Error: ", errorMessage)

    return context.res.text("Check the Clikkle Console to see logs and errors!")
end
```
```deno

    let errorMessage = "This is an error, use for logging errors to console";
```

{% /multicode %}

You can access these logs through the following steps.

1. In Clikkle Console, navigate to Functions.
2. Click to open a function you wish to inspect.
3. Under the Executions tab, click on an execution.
4. In the Response section, you'll be able to view logs under the Logs and Errors tabs.

# Accessing environment variables {% #environment-variables %}
If you need to pass constants or secrets to Clikkle Functions, you can use environment variables.

| Variable                          | Description                                    |	Available at Build and/or Run Time                 |
|-----------------------------------|------------------------------------------------|-----------------------------------------------------|
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_API_ENDPOINT`    |  The API endpoint of the running function      | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_VERSION`                  |  The Clikkle version used to run the function | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_REGION`                   |  The region where the function will run from   | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_API_KEY`         |  The function API key is used for server authentication | Build time                               |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_ID`              |  The ID of the running function.               | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_NAME`            |  The Name of the running function.             | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_DEPLOYMENT`      |  The deployment ID of the running function.    | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID`      |  The project ID of the running function.       | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_RUNTIME_NAME`    |  The runtime of the running function.          | Both                                              |
| `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_RUNTIME_VERSION` |  The runtime version of the running function.  | Both                                              |

{% arrow_link href="/docs/products/functions/functions#environment-variables" %}
Learn to add variables to you function
{% /arrow_link %}

You can access the environment variables through the systems library of each language.

{% multicode %}
```server-nodejs
export default async ({ req, res, log }) => {
    return res.text(process.env.MY_VAR);
}
```
```php
<?php

return function ($context) {
    return $context->res->text(getenv('MY_VAR'));
};
```
```python
def main(context):
    return context.res.text(os.environ['MY_VAR'])
```

# Dependencies {% #dependencies %}
To install your dependencies before your function is built,
you should add the relevant install command to the top your function's **Build setting** > **Commands**.
You can find this setting under **Functions** > your function > **Settings** > **Configuration** > **Build settings**.

Make sure to include dependency files like `package.json`, `composer.json`, `requirements.txt`, etc. in your function's configured [root directory](/docs/products/functions/deploy-from-git#root-directory).
Do not include the dependency folders like `node_modules`, `vendor`, etc. in your function's root directory.
The dependencies installed for your local OS may not work in the executor environments

Your function's dependencies should be managed by the package manager of each language.
By default, we include the following package managers in each runtime.

# Using Clikkle in a function {% #using-clikkle %}
Clikkle can be used in your functions by adding the relevant SDK to your function's dependencies.
Authenticating with Clikkle is done via a dynamic API key or a JWT token.

## Dynamic API key {% #dynamic-api-key %}
Dynamic API keys are the same as [API keys](/docs/advanced/platform/api-keys) but are automatically generated.
They are generated in your functions per execution.
However, you can only use dynamic API keys inside Clikkle functions.

During the build process, dynamic API keys are automatically provided as the environment variable `CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_API_KEY`. This environment variable doesn't need to be initialized.

During execution, dynamic API keys are automatically provided in the `x-clikkle-key` [header](#headers).

Dynamic API keys grant access and operate without sessions.
They allow your function to act as an admin-type role instead of acting on behalf of a user.
Update the function settings to configure the scopes of the function.

1. In Clikkle Console, navigate to **Functions**.
2. Click to open a function you wish to configure.
3. Under the **Settings** tab, navigate to **Scopes**.
4. Select the scopes you want to grant the dynamic key.
5. It is best practice to allow only necessary permissions.

{% multicode %}
```server-nodejs
import { Client, TablesDB, ID } from 'node-clikkle';

export default async ({ req, res, log, error }) => {
    // Set project and set API key
    const client = new Client()
       .setProject(process.env.CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID)
       .setKey(req.headers['x-clikkle-key']);

    const tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

    try {
        await tablesDB.createRow({
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID.unique(),
            data: {}
        })
    } catch (e) {
        error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
        return res.text("Failed to create row")
    }

    return res.text("Row created")
}
```
```php
<?php

require(__DIR__ . '/../vendor/autoload.php');

use Clikkle\Client;
use Clikkle\Exception;
use Clikkle\Services\TablesDB;
use Clikkle\ID;

return function ($context) {
    // Set project and set API key
    $client = (new Client())
        ->setProject(getenv('CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID'))
        ->setKey($context->req->headers['x-clikkle-key']);

    $tablesDB = new TablesDB($client);

    try {
        $tablesDB->createRow(
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID::unique(),
            data: []
        );
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        $context->error("Failed to create row: " . $e->getMessage());
        return $context->res->text("Failed to create row");
    }

    return $context->res->text("Row created");
};
```
```python
from clikkle.client import Client
from clikkle.services.tables_db import TablesDB
from clikkle.id import ID

import os

def main(context):
    # Set project and set API key
    client = (
        Client()
            .set_project(os.environ["CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"])
            .set_key(context.req.headers["x-clikkle-key"])
    )

    tablesDB = TablesDB(client)

    try:
        tablesDB.create_row(
            database_id="<DATABASE_ID>",
            table_id="<TABLE_ID>",
            row_id=ID.unique(),
            data={}
        )
    except Exception as e:
        context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
        return context.response.text("Failed to create row")

    return context.response.text("Row created")
```
```ruby
require "clikkle"

include Clikkle

def main(context)
    # Set project and set API key
    client = Clikkle::Client.new
      .set_project(ENV['CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID'])
      .set_key(context.req.headers['x-clikkle-key'])

    tablesDB = Clikkle::TablesDB.new(client)

    begin
        tablesDB.create_row(
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID.unique(),
            data: {}
        )
    rescue Exception => e
        context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
        return context.response.text("Failed to create row")
    end

    return context.response.text("Row created")
end
```
```deno
import { Client, TablesDB, ID } from "npm:node-clikkle";

export default function ({req, res, error}: any){
    // Set project and set API key
    const client = new Client()
       .setProject(Deno.env.get("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))
       .setKey(req.headers["x-clikkle-key"] || "");

    const tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

    try {
        tablesDB.createRow(
            "<DATABASE_ID>",
            "<TABLE_ID>",
            ID.unique(),
            {}
        );
    } catch (e) {
        error("Failed to create row: " + e.message);
        return res.text("Failed to create row");
    }

    return res.text("Row created");
}
```
```go
package handler

import (
	"fmt"
	"os"

	"github.com/clikkle/sdk-for-go/clikkle"
	"github.com/clikkle/sdk-for-go/id"
	"github.com/open-runtimes/types-for-go/v4/openruntimes"
)

func Main(Context openruntimes.Context) openruntimes.Response {
	// Set project and set API key
	client := clikkle.NewClient(
		clikkle.WithProject(os.Getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID")),
		clikkle.WithKey(Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-key"]),
	)

	databases := clikkle.NewTablesDB(client)

	_, err := databases.createRow(
		"<DATABASE_ID>",
		"<TABLE_ID>",
		id.Unique(),
		map[string]interface{}{},
	)

	if err != nil {
		Context.Log(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to create row: %v", err))
		return Context.Res.Text("Failed to create row")
	}

	return Context.Res.Text("Row created")
}
```

```dart
    final tablesDB = TablesDB(client);

    try {
        await tablesDB.createRow(
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID.unique(),
            data: {}
        );
    } catch (e) {
        context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message);
        return context.res.text("Failed to create row");
    }

    return context.res.text("Row created");
}
```
```swift
import Clikkle
import ClikkleModels
import Foundation

func main(context: RuntimeContext) async throws -> RuntimeOutput {
    // Set project and set API key
    let client = Client()
       .setProject(ProcessInfo.processInfo.environment["CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"])
       .setKey(context.req.headers["x-clikkle-key"] ?? "")

    let tablesDB = TablesDB(client: client)

    do {
        try await tablesDB.createRow(
            databaseId: "<DATABASE_ID>",
            tableId: "<TABLE_ID>",
            rowId: ID.unique(),
            data: [:]
        )
    } catch {
        context.error("Failed to create row: \(error.localizedDescription)")
        return context.res.text("Failed to create row")
    }

    return context.res.text("Row created")
}
```
```csharp
using Clikkle;
using Clikkle.Services;
using Clikkle.Models;

namespace DotNetRuntime
{
    public class Handler
    {
        public async Task Main(RuntimeContext Context)
        {
            // Set API
            var client = new Client()
                .SetProject(Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))
                .SetKey(Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-key"]);

            var tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

            try {
                await databases.createRow(
                    databaseId: "<DATABASE_ID>",
                    tableId: "<TABLE_ID>",
                    rowId: ID.Unique(),
                    data: new Dictionary<string, object>());
            } catch (Exception e) {
                Context.Error("Failed to create row: " + e.Message);
                return Context.Response.Text("Failed to create row");
            }

            return Context.Response.Text("Row created");
        }
    }
}
```

```kotlin
import java.util.HashMap

class Main {
    fun main(context: RuntimeContext): RuntimeOutput {
        // Set project and set API key
        val client = Client()
           .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))
           .setKey(context.req.headers["x-clikkle-key"])

        val tablesDB = TablesDB(client)

        try {
            tablesDB.createRow(
                databaseId = "<DATABASE_ID>",
                tableId = "<TABLE_ID>",
                rowId = ID.unique()
                data = mapOf()
            )
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
            return context.res.text("Failed to create row")
        }

        return context.res.text("Row created")
    }
}
```

```java
package io.openruntimes.java.src;

import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeContext;
import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeOutput;
import java.util.HashMap;
import io.clikkle.Client;

public class Main {
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        // Set project and set API key
        Client client = new Client();
             .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))
             .setKey(context.getReq().getHeaders().get("x-clikkle-key"));

        Databases tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

        try {
            tablesDB.createRow(
                "<DATABASE_ID>",
                "<TABLE_ID>",
                ID.unique(),
                new HashMap<>()
            );
        } catch (Exception e) {
            context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.getMessage());
            return context.res.text("Failed to create row");
        }

        return context.res.text("Row created");
    }
}
```

## Using with JWT {% #using-jwt %}
JWTs allow you to act on behalf of an user in your Clikkle Function.
When using JWTs, you will be able to access and change **only** the resources with the same permissions as the user account that signed the JWT.
This preserves the permissions you configured on each resource.

If the Clikkle Function is invoked by an authenticated user, the `x-clikkle-user-jwt` header is automatically passed in.

{% multicode %}

```server-nodejs
import { Client, TablesDB, ID } from 'node-clikkle';

export default async ({ req, res, log }) => {
    const client = new Client()
        .setProject(process.env.CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID)

    if (req.headers['x-clikkle-user-jwt']) {
        client.setJWT(req.headers['x-clikkle-user-jwt'])
    } else {
        return res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.");
    }

    const tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

    try {
        await tablesDB.createRow({
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID.unique(),
            data: {}
        })
    } catch (e) {
        log("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
        return res.text("Failed to create row")
    }

    return res.text("Row created")
}
```
```php
<?php

require(__DIR__ . '/../vendor/autoload.php');

use Clikkle\Client;
use Clikkle\Exception;
use Clikkle\Services\TablesDB;
use Clikkle\ID;

return function ($context) {
    $client = new (Client())
        ->setProject(getenv('CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID'))

    if (isset($context->req->headers['x-clikkle-user-jwt'])) {
        $client->setJWT($context->req->headers['x-clikkle-user-jwt']);
    } else {
        return $context->res->text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.");
    }

    $tablesDB = new TablesDB($client);

    try {
        $tablesDB->createRow(
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID::unique(),
            data: []
        );
    } catch (Exception $e) {
        $context->error("Failed to create row: " . $e->getMessage());
        return $context->res->text("Failed to create row");
    }

    return $context->res->text("Row created");
};
```
```python
from clikkle.client import Client
from clikkle.services.tables_db import TablesDB
from clikkle.id import ID

import os

def main(context):
    client = (
        Client()
            .set_project(os.environ["CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"])
    )

    if "x-clikkle-user-jwt" in context.req.headers:
        client.set_jwt(context.req.headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"])
    else:
        return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.")

    tablesDB = TablesDB(client)

    try:
        tablesDB.create_row(
            database_id="<DATABASE_ID>",
            table_id="<TABLE_ID>",
            row_id=ID.unique(),
            data={}
        )
    except Exception as e:
```
```ruby
        context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
        return context.response.text("Failed to create row")

    return context.response.text("Row created")
```

```go
package handler

import (
	"fmt"
	"log"

	"github.com/clikkle/sdk-for-go/clikkle"
	"github.com/clikkle/sdk-for-go/id"
	"github.com/open-runtimes/types-for-go/v4/openruntimes"
)

func Main(Context openruntimes.Context) openruntimes.Response {
	client := clikkle.NewClient(
		clikkle.WithProject("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"),
	)

	jwt, exists := Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"]
	if !exists || len(jwt) == 0 {
		clikkle.WithJWT(Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"])
	} else {
		return Context.Res.Text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.")
	}

	databases := clikkle.NewTablesDB(client)

	_, err := databases.createRow(
		"<DATABASE_ID>",
		"<TABLE_ID>",
		id.Unique(),
		map[string]interface{}{},
	)

	if err != nil {
        Context.Log(fmt.Sprintf("Failed to create row: %v", err))
		return Context.Res.Text(str)
	}

	return Context.Res.Text("Row created")
}
```
```dart
import 'dart:io';
import 'dart:async';
import 'package:dart_clikkle/dart_clikkle.dart';

Future<dynamic> main(final context) async {
    final client = Client()
        .setProject(Platform.environment['CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID'])

    if (context.req.headers['x-clikkle-user-jwt'] != null) {
        client.setJWT(context.req.headers['x-clikkle-user-jwt']);
    } else {
        return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.");
    }

    final tablesDB = TablesDB(client);

    try {
        await tablesDB.createRow(
            databaseId: '<DATABASE_ID>',
            tableId: '<TABLE_ID>',
            rowId: ID.unique(),
            data: {}
        );
    } catch (e) {
        context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message);
        return context.res.text("Failed to create row");
    }

    return context.res.text("Row created");
}
```
```swift
import Clikkle
import ClikkleModels
import Foundation

func main(context: RuntimeContext) async throws -> RuntimeOutput {
    let client = Client()
       .setProject(ProcessInfo.processInfo.environment["CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"])

    if let jwt = context.req.headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"] {
        client.setJWT(jwt)
    } else {
        return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.")
    }

    let tablesDB = TablesDB(client: client)

    do {
        try await tablesDB.createRow(
            databaseId: "<DATABASE_ID>",
            tableId: "<TABLE_ID>",
            rowId: ID.unique()
            data: [:]
        )
    } catch {
        context.error("Failed to create row: \(error.localizedDescription)")
        return context.res.text("Failed to create row")
    }

    return context.res.text("Row created")
}
```
```csharp
using Clikkle;
using Clikkle.Services;
using Clikkle.Models;

namespace DotNetRuntime
{
    public class Handler
    {
        public async Task Main(RuntimeContext Context)
        {
            var client = new Client()
               .SetProject(Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))

            if (Context.Req.Headers.ContainsKey("x-clikkle-user-jwt")) {
                client.SetJWT(Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"]);
            } else {
                return Context.Res.Text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue");
            }

            var tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

            try {
                await databases.createRow(
                    databaseId: "<DATABASE_ID>",
                    tableId: "<TABLE_ID>",
                    rowId: ID.Unique(),
                    data: new Dictionary<string, object>());
            } catch (Exception e) {
                Context.Error("Failed to create row: " + e.Message);
                return Context.Res.Text("Failed to create row");
            }

            return Context.Res.Text("Row created");
        }
    }
}
```
```kotlin
package io.openruntimes.kotlin.src

import io.openruntimes.kotlin.RuntimeContext
import io.openruntimes.kotlin.RuntimeOutput
import io.clikkle.Client
import io.clikkle.services.TablesDB
import io.clikkle.ID
import java.util.HashMap

class Main {
    fun main(context: RuntimeContext): RuntimeOutput {
        val client = Client()
           .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))

        if (context.req.headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"] != null) {
            client.setJWT(context.req.headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"])
        } else {
            return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.")
        }

        val tablesDB = TablesDB(client)

        try {
            tablesDB.createRow(
                databaseId = "<DATABASE_ID>",
                tableId = "<TABLE_ID>",
                rowId = ID.unique(),
                data = mapOf()
            )
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
            return context.res.text("Failed to create row")
        }

        return context.res.text("Row created")
    }
}
```

```java
package io.openruntimes.java.src;

import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeContext;
import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeOutput;
import java.util.HashMap;
import io.clikkle.Client;

public class Main {
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        Client client = new Client()
            .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))

        if (context.req.headers.containsKey("x-clikkle-user-jwt")) {
            client.setJWT(context.req.headers.get("x-clikkle-user-jwt"));
        } else {
            return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.");
        }

        Databases tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

        try {
            tablesDB.createRow(
                "<DATABASE_ID>",
                "<TABLE_ID>",
                ID.unique(),
                new HashMap<>()
            );
        } catch (Exception e) {
            context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.getMessage());
            return context.res.text("Failed to create row");
        }

        return context.res.text("Row created");

    }
}
```

# Code structure {% #code-structure %}

As your functions grow, you may find yourself needing to split your code into multiple files. This helps you keep your codebase maintainable and easy to read. Here's how you can accomplish code splitting.

{% tabs %}
{% tabsitem #nodejs title="Node.js" %}
```server-nodejs
// src/utils.js
export function add(a, b) {
    return a + b;
}
```
```server-nodejs
// src/main.js
import { add } from './utils.js';

export default function ({ res }) {
    return res.text(add(1, 2));
}
```
{% /tabsitem %}

{% tabsitem #php title="PHP" %}
```php
<?php
// src/utils.php
function add($a, $b) {
    return $a + $b;
}
```
```php
<?php
// src/main.php
require_once(__DIR__ . '/utils.php');

return function ($context) {
    return $context->res->text(add(1, 2));
};
```
{% /tabsitem %}

{% tabsitem #python title="Python" %}
```python
# src/utils.py
def add(a, b):
    return a + b
```
```python
# src/main.py
from .utils import add

def main(context):
    return context.res.text(add(1, 2))
```
{% /tabsitem %}

{% tabsitem #ruby title="Ruby" %}
```ruby
# lib/utils.rb
def add(a, b)
    return a + b
end
```
```ruby
# lib/main.rb
require_relative 'utils'

def main(context)
    return context.res.text(add(1, 2))
end
```
{% /tabsitem %}

{% tabsitem #deno title="Deno" %}
```deno
// src/utils.ts
export function add(a: number, b: number): number {
    return a + b;
}
```
```deno
// src/main.ts
import { add } from './utils.ts';

export default function ({res}: {res: any}) {
    return res.text(add(1, 2));
}
```
{% /tabsitem %}

{% tabsitem #go title="Go" %}
```go
// src/utils/go.mod
module example.com/utils

go 1.23.0
```
```go
// src/utils/utils.go
package utils

func Add(a int, b int) int {
	return a + b
}
```
```go
// src/main/go.mod
module example.com/main

go 1.23.0

replace example.com/utils => ../utils // Run go mod edit -replace example.com/go=../go

require example.com/utils v0.0.0-00010101000000-000000000000 // Run go mod tidy
```
```go
// src/main/main.go
package main

import "example.com/utils"

func main() {
	// Get a greeting message and print it.
	message := utils.Add(5, 4)
	print(message)
}
```
{% /tabsitem %}

```dart
// lib/utils.dart

    return a + b;
}
```
```dart
// lib/main.dart
import 'dart:async';

import 'package:package_name/utils.dart';

Future<dynamic> main(final context) async {
    return context.res.text(add(1, 2));
```
```java
}
```
{% /tabsitem %}

use Clikkle\Client;
use Clikkle\Exception;

// This is your Clikkle function
// It's executed each time we get a request
return function ($context) {
    // Why not try the Clikkle SDK?
    //
    // Set project and set API key
    // $client = (new Client())
    //      ->setProject(getenv(CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID))
    //      ->setKey($context->req->headers['x-clikkle-key']);
   
    // You can log messages to the console
    $context->log('Hello, Logs!');

    // If something goes wrong, log an error
    $context->error('Hello, Errors!');

    // The `req` object contains the request data
    if ($context->req->method === 'GET') {
        // Send a response with the res object helpers
        // `res.text()` dispatches a string back to the client
        return $context->res->text('Hello, World!');
    }

    // `res.json()` is a handy helper for sending JSON
    return $context->res->json([
        'motto' => 'Build like a team of hundreds_',
        'learn' => 'https://clikkle.io/docs',
        'connect' => 'https://clikkle.io/discord',
        'getInspired' => 'https://builtwith.clikkle.io',
    ]);
};

	"github.com/clikkle/sdk-for-go/clikkle"

type Response struct {
	Motto       string `json:"motto"`
	Learn       string `json:"learn"`
	Connect     string `json:"connect"`
	GetInspired string `json:"getInspired"`
}

func Main(Context openruntimes.Context) openruntimes.Response {
	// This is your Clikkle function
	// It's executed each time we get a request service
	var _ = clikkle.NewClient(
		clikkle.WithProject(os.Getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID")),
		clikkle.WithKey(Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-key"]),
	)

	// You can log messages to the console
	fmt.Println("Hello, Logs!")

	fmt.Fprintln(os.Stderr, "Error:", "Hello, Errors!")

	// The `Context.Req` object contains the request data
	if Context.Req.Method == "GET" {
		// Send a response with the Context.Res object helpers
		// `Context.Res.Text()` dispatches a string back to the client
		return Context.Res.Text("Hello, World!")
	}

	// `res.json()` is a handy helper for sending JSON

		Response{
			Motto:       "Build like a team of hundreds_",
			Learn:       "https://clikkle.io/docs",
			Connect:     "https://clikkle.io/discord",
			GetInspired: "https://builtwith.clikkle.io",
		})
}

69:T609,package io.openruntimes.java.src;

import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeContext;
import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeOutput;
import java.util.HashMap;
import io.clikkle.Client;

public class Main {

    // This is your Clikkle function
    // It's executed each time we get a request
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        // Why not try the Clikkle SDK?
        //
        // Set project and set API key
        // Client client = new Client();
        //     .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))
        //     .setKey(context.getReq().getHeaders().get("x-clikkle-key"));

        // You can log messages to the console
        context.log("Hello, Logs!");

        // If something goes wrong, log an error
        context.error("Hello, Errors!");

        // The `context.getReq()` object contains the request data
        if (context.getReq().getMethod().equals("GET")) {
            // Send a response with the res object helpers
            // `context.getRes().text()` dispatches a string back to the client
            return context.getRes().text("Hello, World!");
        }

        Map json = new HashMap<>();
        json.put("motto", "Build like a team of hundreds_");
        json.put("learn", "https://clikkle.io/docs");
        json.put("connect", "https://clikkle.io/discord");
        json.put("getInspired", "https://builtwith.clikkle.io");

        // `context.getRes().json()` is a handy helper for sending JSON
        return context.getRes().json(json);
    }
}

// This is your Clikkle function

func main(context: RuntimeContext) async throws -> RuntimeOutput {

    //    .setProject(ProcessInfo.processInfo.environment["CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"])

    // If something goes wrong, log an error

71:T4dd,export default async ({ req, res, log }) => {
    log(req.bodyText);                    // Raw request body, contains request data
    log(JSON.stringify(req.bodyJson));    // Object from parsed JSON request body, otherwise string
    log(JSON.stringify(req.headers));     // String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    log(req.scheme);                      // Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    log(req.method);                      // Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    log(req.url);                         // Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    log(req.host);                        // Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io
    log(req.port);                        // Port from the host header, for example 8000
    log(req.path);                        // Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks
    log(req.queryString);                 // Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"
    log(JSON.stringify(req.query));       // Parsed query params. For example, req.query.limit

    return res.text("All the request parameters are logged to the Clikkle Console.");
};

    log(req.url);                         // Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50

    log(req.port);                        // Port from the host header, for example 8000

    log(req.queryString);                 // Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"

return function ($context) {
    $context->log(json_encode($context->req->bodyJson));// Object from parsed JSON request body, otherwise string
    $context->log(json_encode($context->req->headers)); // String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    $context->log($context->req->scheme);               // Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    $context->log($context->req->method);               // Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    $context->log($context->req->url);                  // Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    $context->log($context->req->host);                 // Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io
    $context->log($context->req->port);                 // Port from the host header, for example 8000
    $context->log($context->req->path);                 // Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks
    $context->log($context->req->queryString);          // Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"
    $context->log(json_encode($context->req->query));   // Parsed query params. For example, req.query.limit

    return $context->res->text("All the request parameters are logged to the Clikkle Console.");
}

    $context->log(json_encode($context->req->headers)); // String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    $context->log($context->req->scheme);               // Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https

c4:T52b,import json

def main(context):
    context.log(context.req.body_text)             # Raw request body, contains request data
    context.log(json.dumps(context.req.body_json)) # Object from parsed JSON request body, otherwise string
    context.log(json.dumps(context.req.headers))   # String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    context.log(context.req.scheme)                # Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    context.log(context.req.method)                # Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    context.log(context.req.url)                   # Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    context.log(context.req.host)                  # Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io
    context.log(context.req.port)                  # Port from the host header, for example 8000
    context.log(context.req.path)                  # Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks
    context.log(context.req.query_string)          # Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"
    context.log(json.dumps(context.req.query))     # Parsed query params. For example, req.query.limit

    return context.res.text("All the request parameters are logged to the Clikkle Console.")

def main(context)
    context.log(context.req.body_text)                #  Raw request body, contains request data
    context.log(JSON.generate(context.req.body_json)) # Object from parsed JSON request body, otherwise string
    context.log(JSON.generate(context.req.headers))   # String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    context.log(context.req.scheme)                   # Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    context.log(context.req.method)                   # Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    context.log(context.req.url)                      # Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    context.log(context.req.host)                     # Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io
    context.log(context.req.port)                     # Port from the host header, for example 8000
    context.log(context.req.path)                     # Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks
    context.log(context.req.query_string)             # Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"
    context.log(JSON.generate(context.req.query))     # Parsed query params. For example, req.query.limit

    return context.res.text("All the request parameters are logged to the Clikkle Console.")

    context.log(context.req.scheme)                   # Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    context.log(context.req.method)                   # Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    context.log(context.req.url)                      # Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    context.log(context.req.host)                     # Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io

    context.log(context.req.query_string)             # Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"

c8:T4cb,export default async ({ req, res, log }: any) => {
    log(req.bodyText);                  // Raw request body, contains request data
    log(JSON.stringify(req.bodyJson));  // Object from parsed JSON request body, otherwise string
    log(JSON.stringify(req.headers));   // String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    log(req.scheme);                    // Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    log(req.method);                    // Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    log(req.url);                       // Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    log(req.host);                      // Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io
    log(req.port);                      // Port from the host header, for example 8000
    log(req.path);                      // Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks
    log(req.queryString);               // Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"
    log(JSON.stringify(req.query));     // Parsed query params. For example, req.query.limit

    return res.text("All the request parameters are logged to the Clikkle Console.");
}
c9:T4cb,export default async ({ req, res, log }: any) => {
    log(req.bodyText);                  // Raw request body, contains request data
    log(JSON.stringify(req.bodyJson));  // Object from parsed JSON request body, otherwise string
    log(JSON.stringify(req.headers));   // String key-value pairs of all request headers, keys are lowercase
    log(req.scheme);                    // Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    log(req.method);                    // Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    log(req.url);                       // Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    log(req.host);                      // Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io
    log(req.port);                      // Port from the host header, for example 8000
    log(req.path);                      // Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks
    log(req.queryString);               // Raw query params string. For example "limit=12&offset=50"
    log(JSON.stringify(req.query));     // Parsed query params. For example, req.query.limit

    return res.text("All the request parameters are logged to the Clikkle Console.");

func main(context: RuntimeContext) async throws -> RuntimeOutput {

    context.log(context.req.scheme)                                                        // Value of the x-forwarded-proto header, usually http or https
    context.log(context.req.method)                                                        // Request method, such as GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, PATCH, etc.
    context.log(context.req.url)                                                           // Full URL, for example: http://awesome.clikkle.io:8000/v1/hooks?limit=12&offset=50
    context.log(context.req.host)                                                          // Hostname from the host header, such as awesome.clikkle.io

    context.log(context.req.path)                                                          // Path part of URL, for example /v1/hooks

    }

d6:T438,package io.openruntimes.java.src;

import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeContext;
import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeOutput;
import java.util.Map;
import java.util.HashMap;

public class Main {
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        switch (context.getReq().getQuery()["type"]) {
            case "text":
                return context.getRes().empty();
            case "json":
                HashMap<String, Object> data = new HashMap<>();
                data.put("type", "This is a JSON response");
                return context.getRes().text(data);
            case "binary"
                return context.getRes().binary(Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get("file.png")));
            case "redirect":
                return context.getRes().redirect("https://clikkle.io", 301);
            case "html":
                return context.getRes().text("<h1>This is an HTML response</h1>", 200, Map.of("content-type", "text/html"));
            default:
                return context.getRes().text("This is a text response");
        }
    }
}

import io.openruntimes.java.RuntimeContext;

public class Main {
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        switch (context.getReq().getQuery()["type"]) {
            case "text":
                return context.getRes().empty();
            case "json":
                HashMap<String, Object> data = new HashMap<>();
                data.put("type", "This is a JSON response");
                return context.getRes().text(data);
            case "binary"
                return context.getRes().binary(Files.readAllBytes(Paths.get("file.png")));
            case "redirect":
                return context.getRes().redirect("https://clikkle.io", 301);
            case "html":
                return context.getRes().text("<h1>This is an HTML response</h1>", 200, Map.of("content-type", "text/html"));
            default:
                return context.getRes().text("This is a text response");
        }
    }
}
8b:["$","$L11",null,{"language":"java","content":"$d6","children":"$d7"}]
d8:T46a,#include "../RuntimeResponse.h"
#include "../RuntimeRequest.h"
#include "../RuntimeOutput.h"
#include "../RuntimeContext.h"

namespace runtime {
  class Handler {
    public:
      static RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext &context) {
        std::string type = context.req.query["type"];

        if (type == "empty") {
          return context.res.empty();
        } else if (type == "json") {
          Json::Value data;
          data["type"] = "This is a JSON response";
          return context.res.text(data);
        } else if (type == "binary") {
          std::vector<char> buffer(std::istreambuf_iterator<char>(std::ifstream("file.png", std::ios::binary)), {});
          return context.res.binary(buffer)
        } else if (type == "redirect") {
          return context.res.redirect("https://clikkle.io", 301);
        } else if (type == "html") {
          Json::Value headers;
          headers["content-type"] = "text/html";
          return context.res.text("<h1>This is an HTML response</h1>", 200, headers);
        } else {
          return context.res.text("This is a text response");
        }
      }
  };
}

namespace runtime {
  class Handler {
    public:
      static RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext &context) {
        std::string type = context.req.query["type"];

        if (type == "empty") {
          return context.res.empty();
        } else if (type == "json") {
          Json::Value data;
          data["type"] = "This is a JSON response";
          return context.res.text(data);
        } else if (type == "binary") {
          std::vector<char> buffer(std::istreambuf_iterator<char>(std::ifstream("file.png", std::ios::binary)), {});
          return context.res.binary(buffer)
        } else if (type == "redirect") {
          return context.res.redirect("https://clikkle.io", 301);
        } else if (type == "html") {
          Json::Value headers;
          headers["content-type"] = "text/html";
          return context.res.text("<h1>This is an HTML response</h1>", 200, headers);
        } else {
          return context.res.text("This is a text response");
        }
      }
  };
}

da:T4a0,using Clikkle;
using Clikkle.Services;
using Clikkle.Models;

namespace DotNetRuntime
{
    public class Handler
    {
        public async Task Main(RuntimeContext Context)
        {
            var client = new Client()
               .SetProject(Environment.GetEnvironmentVariable("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))

            if (Context.Req.Headers.ContainsKey("x-clikkle-user-jwt")) {
                client.SetJWT(Context.Req.Headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"]);
            } else {
                return Context.Res.Text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue");
            }

            var tablesDB = new TablesDB(client);

            try {
                await databases.createRow(
                    databaseId: "<DATABASE_ID>",
                    tableId: "<TABLE_ID>",
                    rowId: ID.Unique(),
                    data: new Dictionary<string, object>());
            } catch (Exception e) {
                Context.Error("Failed to create row: " + e.Message);
                return Context.Res.Text("Failed to create row");
            }

            return Context.Res.Text("Row created");
        }
    }
}

dc:T48a,package io.openruntimes.kotlin.src

import io.openruntimes.kotlin.RuntimeContext
import io.openruntimes.kotlin.RuntimeOutput
import io.clikkle.Client
import io.clikkle.services.TablesDB
import io.clikkle.ID
import java.util.HashMap

class Main {
    fun main(context: RuntimeContext): RuntimeOutput {
        val client = Client()
           .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))

        if (context.req.headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"] != null) {
            client.setJWT(context.req.headers["x-clikkle-user-jwt"])
        } else {
            return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.")
        }

        val tablesDB = TablesDB(client)

        try {
            tablesDB.createRow(
                databaseId = "<DATABASE_ID>",
                tableId = "<TABLE_ID>",
                rowId = ID.unique(),
                data = mapOf()
            )
        } catch (e: Exception) {
            context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.message)
            return context.res.text("Failed to create row")
        }

        return context.res.text("Row created")
    }
}

public class Main {
    public RuntimeOutput main(RuntimeContext context) throws Exception {
        Client client = new Client()
            .setProject(System.getenv("CLIKKLE_FUNCTION_PROJECT_ID"))

        if (context.req.headers.containsKey("x-clikkle-user-jwt")) {
            client.setJWT(context.req.headers.get("x-clikkle-user-jwt"));
        } else {
            return context.res.text("Access denied: This function requires authentication. Please sign in to continue.");
        }

        try {
            tablesDB.createRow(
                "<DATABASE_ID>",
                "<TABLE_ID>",
                ID.unique(),
                new HashMap<>()
            );
        } catch (Exception e) {
            context.error("Failed to create row: " + e.getMessage());
            return context.res.text("Failed to create row");
        }

        return context.res.text("Row created");

    }
}
